#  recipe to execute (from 'Makefile', line 46):
	@mkdir -p $(BUILD_PATH)
	@set -e; rm -f $@; \
	$(CC) -M $(CFLAGS) $(CPLEXFLAGS) $< > $@.$$$$; \
	sed 's,\($*\)\.o[ :]*,\1.o $@ : ,g' < $@.$$$$ > $@; \
	rm -f $@.$$$$
